#### Gemini Predictions

How to make a prediction

#### Pick a market

Browse available event contracts. Each one is a clear yes/no question tied to a real-world outcome.

#### Choose your position

Select Yes or No and place your order. You can adjust or sell your position any time before the event closes, subject to market availability.

#### Get paid out

If your prediction is correct when the event resolves, you receive $1.00 per contract, automatically credited to your Gemini account.

[

Get started

](https://exchange.gemini.com/register)

The stability of a stablecoin is dependent on the value and stability of the underlying asset and the transparency and auditability of the stablecoin’s issuer, among other risks which may be unique to individual stablecoins. Depegging events may occur with stablecoins that fail to maintain adequate controls and risk mitigants. A depegging event is when the value of the stablecoin no longer matches the value of the underlying asset.
